4a4(2): khsam gtan mkha' grong yo shes dbyings// 'dod yin la sogs dga' 'phrod la phyi nang btun la/ ye shes rgyun mi gcad par dbab/ klong 'gyur bsam gtan mkha' klong ye shes

4b1(2): yin/ bsam gtan mkha' kling ye shes dbyings su 'das pa yod/ ye shes me chen nyon mongs shing la sar/ ma go ba la rtag tu smra la gdab/ lhan cig skyes pa'i rang bzhin de//
